qt-examples in fedora-rawhide

This page displays detail informations of the qt-examples package. You might want go back to the main page of qt-examples.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2020-08-19 Kevin Kofler - 4.8.7-57 - Hardcode the compiler version in the build key once and for all
2020-08-19 Jeff Law - 4.8.7-56 - Add support for gcc-11 - Fix ordered pointer comparison against zero problems
2020-08-13 Than Ngo - 4.8.7-55 - fixed #1868534 - CVE-2020-17507
2020-07-29 Fedora Release Engineering - 1:4.8.7-54 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_33_Mass_Rebuild
2020-07-01 Jeff Law - 4.8.7-53 - Disable LTO
2020-01-31 Than Ngo - 4.8.7-52 - fixed FTBFS against gcc10
2020-01-30 Fedora Release Engineering - 1:4.8.7-51 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_32_Mass_Rebuild
